***capisce.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:capisce.html>capisce</a> (70692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed (<a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:change.html>change</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spelling.html>spelling</a> reflecting <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pronunciation.html>pronunciation</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:capisci.html>capisci</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> second-person singular <a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:indicative.html>indicative</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">capire</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:understand.html>understand</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:through.html>through</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:vulgar.html>Vulgar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*capīre</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">capere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grasp.html>grasp</a>, <a href = class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Italic language">Proto-Italic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="itc-pro">*kapiō</i>, <a vnd.unilang:root.html>root</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*keh₂p-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grab.html>grab</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:seize.html>seize</a></span><span </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection"><a href = vnd.unilang:interjection.html>Interjection</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:capisce.html>capisce</a>?</strong>
</p>
